Excluding working capital effects, cash flow from operations in first quarter 2020 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$5.8 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$6.3 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the corresponding 2019 period. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">CAPITAL AND EXPLORATORY EXPENDITURES</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:12px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Capital and exploratory expenditures in the first three months of 2020 were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.4 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.7 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in 2019.
